     CSR         SARVGN    BEGSR
      *================================================================
      * Upd Push TO Records   RT - Hog Voucher Detail  * 
      *================================================================
      *
     C                     MOVEL*BLANK    WN0001  1        Push Status
      *
     C                     MOVEL*BLANK    W0RTN   7
      * USER: Initialize routine
      * Note: This RTVOBJ is built over an Access Path that only selects
      *       records where the Push Payment Status is either blank, or i
      *       "N".  This was done to speed up the push process.
      * Declare restrictor key work fields
     C           *LIKE     DEFN WAHMNB    WQSA01           BOH Company Num
      * Define keylist
     C           KRSSA     KLIST
     C                     KFLD           WQSA01           BOH Company Num
      * Setup key
     C                     Z-ADDP1Y8A1    WQSA01           BOH Company Num
      * Establish starting position
     C           KRSSA     SETLL@BLCPXY                    *
     C           KRSSA     READE@BLCPXY                  90*
      * Data record not found
     C   90                MOVEL'PRK0101' W0RTN   7
     C           *IN90     DOWEQ'0'
      * USER: Process Data record
      * Move Push Payment Status to Push Status
     C                     MOVELWAJQST    WN0001           Push Status
      * Only process Triumph Owned records
      * CASE: DB1.VCD Source Code is Triumph Member (Owner)
     C           WAOTCD    IFEQ 'TO'                       *IF
      * Check Push Type and Repayment flag
      * CASE: Push Type = Manual AND Repayment Flag <> Repayment
      *  - c1 AND NOTc2
      *   |- c1    : PAR.Push Type is Manual
      *   |- c2    : DB1.VCD Repayment Flag is Repayment
      *   '-
     C                     MOVEL'0'       Y0CX01  1
     C           P3KTSS    IFEQ 'M'                        *IF
     C           WAC4SS    IFEQ 'R'                        *IF
     C                     ELSE
     C                     MOVEL'1'       Y0CX01
     C                     END                             *FI
     C                     END                             *FI
     C           Y0CX01    IFEQ '1'                        *IF
     C                     MOVELWAJQST    YL0001           Push Status
     C                     ELSE
      * CASE: Push Type = Auto AND Repayment Flag = Repayment
      *  - c1 AND c2
      *   |- c1    : PAR.Push Type is Automatic
      *   |- c2    : DB1.VCD Repayment Flag is Repayment
      *   '-
     C                     MOVEL'0'       Y0CX01  1
     C           P3KTSS    IFEQ 'A'                        *IF
     C           WAC4SS    IFEQ 'R'                        *IF
     C                     MOVEL'1'       Y0CX01
     C                     END                             *FI
     C                     END                             *FI
     C           Y0CX01    IFEQ '1'                        *IF
     C                     MOVELWAJQST    YL0001           Push Status
     C                     ELSE
      * CASE: *OTHERWISE
      * If Producer or Location changes, check Xref file for overrides
      * CASE: If Producer Code OR Location Code values are blank
      *  - c1 OR c2
      *   |- c1    : DB1.PD Producer Code is Blank
      *   |- c2    : DB1.PL Location Code is Blank
      *   '-
     C           WAABCD    IFEQ *BLANK                     *IF
     C           WAAECD    OREQ *BLANK                     *OR
     C                     MOVEL*BLANK    YL0002           Producer Code
     C                     MOVEL*BLANK    YL0003           Location Code U
     C                     MOVEL'N'       YL0004           Process Flag Us
     C                     MOVELWAJQST    YL0001           Push Status
     C                     ELSE
      * CASE: If Producer Code OR Location Code values change
      *  - c1 OR c2
      *   |- c1    : DB1.PD Producer Code NE LCL.Producer Code         US
      *   |- c2    : DB1.PL Location Code NE LCL.Location Code USR
      *   '-
     C           WAABCD    IFNE YL0002                     *IF
     C           WAAECD    ORNE YL0003                     *OR
     C                     MOVELWAABCD    YL0002           Producer Code
     C                     MOVELWAAECD    YL0003           Location Code U
     C                     MOVEL'Y'       YL0004           Process Flag Us
      * Rtv From Vals for To  RT - Producer Location From/TO  * Active rc
     C                     EXSR SBRVGN
      * If Producer Location From/TO record found, check values
      * CASE: LCL.Producer From is Entered
     C           YL0005    IFNE *BLANK                     *IF
      * If From and To values are different, then override from value
      * CASE: Producer Code OR Producer Location values differ
      *  - c1 OR c2
      *   |- c1    : DB1.PD Producer Code NE LCL.Producer From
      *   |- c2    : DB1.PL Location Code NE LCL.Producer Location From
      *   '-
     C           WAABCD    IFNE YL0005                     *IF
     C           WAAECD    ORNE YL0006                     *OR
     C                     MOVELYL0005    YL0007           PD Producer Cod
     C                     MOVELYL0006    YL0008           PL Location Cod
     C                     ELSE
      * CASE: *OTHERWISE
     C                     MOVELWAABCD    YL0007           PD Producer Cod
     C                     MOVELWAAECD    YL0008           PL Location Cod
     C                     END                             *FI
     C                     ELSE
      * CASE: *OTHERWISE
     C                     MOVEL'N'       YL0004           Process Flag Us
     C                     MOVEL'I'       YL0001           Push Status
     C                     END                             *FI
     C                     END                             *FI
     C                     END                             *FI
      * If Process Flag is Yes, perform updates
      * CASE: LCL.Process Flag User is Yes
     C           YL0004    IFEQ 'Y'                        *IF
      * When Buy Order Number changes value
      * CASE: DB1.BOH Buy Order Number NE LCL.BOH Buy Order Number
     C           WABNNB    IFNE YL0009                     *IF
     C                     Z-ADDWABNNB    YL0009           BOH Buy Order N
     C                     Z-ADD*ZERO     YL0010           BOL Load Number
     C                     Z-ADD*ZERO     YL0011           TH Tattoo Numbe
     C                     Z-ADD*ZERO     YL0012           TH Kill Date
      * Rtv Pricing Date by BO RT - Tattoo Header  * Pricing Date
     C                     EXSR SCRVGN
      * If Pricing Date = 0, use Kill Date
      * CASE: LCL.TH Pricing Date is Not Entered
     C           YL0013    IFEQ 0                          *IF
     C                     Z-ADDWAB0DT    YL0013           TH Pricing Date
     C                     END                             *FI
      * The PD Producer Code and PL Location Code values come from the
      * Xref file Producer Location From/TO file using the from values.
      * Upd Push TO Records   RT - Buy Order Header  * 
     C                     EXSR SDRVGN
     C                     END                             *FI
      * When Load Number changes value
      * CASE: DB1.BOL Load Number NE LCL.BOL Load Number
     C           WABONB    IFNE YL0010                     *IF
     C                     Z-ADDWABONB    YL0010           BOL Load Number
     C                     Z-ADD*ZERO     YL0011           TH Tattoo Numbe
     C                     Z-ADD*ZERO     YL0012           TH Kill Date
      * Upd Push TO Records   RT - Buy Order Load  * 
     C                     EXSR SJRVGN
      * Upd Push TO Records   RT - Buy Order Load Weight  * 
     C                     EXSR SMRVGN
     C                     END                             *FI
      * When Tattoo Number OR Kill Date changes value
      * CASE: Tattoo Number OR Kill Date change value
      *  - c1 OR c2
      *   |- c1    : DB1.TH Tattoo Number NE LCL.TH Tattoo Number
      *   |- c2    : DB1.TH Kill Date NE LCL.TH Kill Date
      *   '-
     C           WACVNB    IFNE YL0011                     *IF
     C           WAB0DT    ORNE YL0012                     *OR
     C                     Z-ADDWACVNB    YL0011           TH Tattoo Numbe
     C                     Z-ADDWAB0DT    YL0012           TH Kill Date
      * Upd Push TO Records   RT - Tattoo Header  * 
     C                     EXSR SPRVGN
      * Upd Push TO Records   RT - Tattoo Header EXT  * 
     C                     EXSR STRVGN
      * Upd Push TO Records   RT - Tattoo Detail  * 
     C                     EXSR SWRVGN
      * Dlt Push TO Records   RT - Tattoo Ded/Add  * Delete on Push To si
     C                     EXSR SZRVGN
      * Upd Push TO Records   RT - Tattoo Defect  * 
     C                     EXSR TBRVGN
      * Upd Push TO Records   RT - Tattoo Scale Ticket  * 
     C                     EXSR TERVGN
      * Dlt Push TO Records   RT - Eval Trans  * Delete on Push To side
     C                     EXSR THRVGN
      * Upd Push TO Records   RT - Eval Trans  * 
     C                     EXSR TJRVGN
      * Dlt Push TO Records   RT - Loss Trans  * Delete on Push To side
     C                     EXSR TMRVGN
      * Upd Push TO Records   RT - Loss Trans  * 
     C                     EXSR TORVGN
      * Dlt Carcass Detail    RT - Carcass Detail  * Delete on Push To si
     C                     EXSR TRRVGN
     C                     END                             *FI
     C                     MOVEL'P'       YL0001           Push Status
     C                     END                             *FI
     C                     END                             *FI
     C                     END                             *FI
     C                     ELSE
      * CASE: *OTHERWISE
     C                     MOVEL'I'       YL0001           Push Status
     C                     END                             *FI
     C                     MOVELYL0001    YL0026           VCD Push Paymen
      * Chg Voucher Detail    CH - Hog Voucher Detail  * Unused Status 1=
     C                     EXSR TTCHRC

     C                     ENDDO
      *================================================================
